\doxysubsection{函数说明}
\Hypertarget{namespacecudf_a8bd44b61ff4585b5278f2d2203c909b7}\label{namespacecudf_a8bd44b61ff4585b5278f2d2203c909b7} 
\index{cudf@{cudf}!bit\_cast@{bit\_cast}}
\index{bit\_cast@{bit\_cast}!cudf@{cudf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{bit\_cast()}{bit\_cast()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} cudf\+::bit\+\_\+cast (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} const \&}]{input,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1data__type}{data\+\_\+type}}}]{type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Zero-\/copy cast between types with the same size and compatible underlying representations. 

This is similar to {\ttfamily reinterpret\+\_\+cast} or {\ttfamily bit\+\_\+cast} in that it gives a view of the same raw bits as a different type. Unlike {\ttfamily reinterpret\+\_\+cast} however, this cast is only allowed on types that have the same width and compatible representations. For example, the way timestamp types are laid out in memory is equivalent to an integer representing a duration since a fixed epoch; bit-\/casting to the same integer type (INT32 for days, INT64 for others) results in a raw view of the duration count. A FLOAT32 can also be bit-\/casted into INT32 and treated as an integer value. However, an INT32 column cannot be bit-\/casted to INT64 as the sizes differ, nor can a \doxylink{classcudf_1_1string__view}{string\+\_\+view} column be casted into a numeric type column as their data representations are not compatible.

The validity of the conversion can be checked with {\ttfamily \doxylink{group__utility__types_ga73dd2d74b0eafb1543eb1cd27accd38e}{cudf\+::is\+\_\+bit\+\_\+castable()}}.


\begin{DoxyExceptions}{异常}
{\em \doxylink{structcudf_1_1logic__error}{cudf\+::logic\+\_\+error}} & if the specified cast is not possible, i.\+e., {\ttfamily is\+\_\+bit\+\_\+castable(input.\+type(), type)} is false.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em input} & The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} to cast from \\
\hline
{\em type} & The {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1data__type}{data\+\_\+type}} to cast to \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
New {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} wrapping the same data as {\ttfamily input} but cast to {\ttfamily type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Unlike {\ttfamily reinterpret\+\_\+cast} however, this cast is only allowed on types that have the same width and compatible representations. For example, the way timestamp types are laid out in memory is equivalent to an integer representing a duration since a fixed epoch; bit-\/casting to the same integer type (INT32 for days, INT64 for others) results in a raw view of the duration count. A FLOAT32 can also be bit-\/casted into INT32 and treated as an integer value. \Hypertarget{namespacecudf_a840f61a0eccd339fd42fc7c12e02dbe3}\label{namespacecudf_a840f61a0eccd339fd42fc7c12e02dbe3} 
\index{cudf@{cudf}!column\_types\_equal@{column\_types\_equal}}
\index{column\_types\_equal@{column\_types\_equal}!cudf@{cudf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{column\_types\_equal()}{column\_types\_equal()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily bool cudf\+::column\+\_\+types\+\_\+equal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} const \&}]{lhs,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} const \&}]{rhs }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Compares the type of two {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}}s 

This function returns true if the type of {\ttfamily lhs} equals that of {\ttfamily rhs}.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item For fixed point types, the scale is compared.
\item For dictionary types, the type of the keys are compared if both are non-\/empty columns.
\item For lists types, the type of child columns are compared recursively.
\item For struct types, the type of each field are compared in order.
\item For all other types, the {\ttfamily id} of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1data__type}{data\+\_\+type}} is compared.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em lhs} & The first {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} to compare \\
\hline
{\em rhs} & The second {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcudf_1_1column__view}{column\+\_\+view}} to compare \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
true if column types match 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{namespacecudf_ab3eece7be385b3be2bda53b24a48dbdc}\label{namespacecudf_ab3eece7be385b3be2bda53b24a48dbdc}

\index{scatter\_columns@{scatter\_columns}!cudf@{cudf}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{scatter\_columns()}{scatter\_columns()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1table__view}{table\+\_\+view}} cudf\+::scatter\+\_\+columns (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1table__view}{table\+\_\+view}} const \&}]{source,  }\item[{std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{group__utility__types_ga0aff16b2db009d92300befaca11827e9}{size\+\_\+type}} $>$ const \&}]{map,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcudf_1_1table__view}{table\+\_\+view}} const \&}]{target }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Copy column\+\_\+views from a \doxylink{classcudf_1_1table__view}{table\+\_\+view} into another \doxylink{classcudf_1_1table__view}{table\+\_\+view} according to a column indices map. 

The output table view, {\ttfamily out\+\_\+table} is a copy of the {\ttfamily target} \doxylink{classcudf_1_1table__view}{table\+\_\+view} but with elements updated according to {\ttfamily out\+\_\+table\mbox{[}map\mbox{[}i\mbox{]}\mbox{]} = source\mbox{[}i\mbox{]}} where {\ttfamily i} is {\ttfamily \mbox{[}0,source.\+size())}


\begin{DoxyParams}{参数}
{\em source} & Table of new columns to scatter into the output table view. \\
\hline
{\em map} & The indices where each new\+\_\+column should be copied into the output. \\
\hline
{\em target} & Table to receive the updated column views. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{返回}
